 Under this, chat backup of whatsapp in Google Drive will be given by default

 google ke saath kii gai partnership ke tahat google drive par watsap chats kaa byaap rakhane se aapako die gaye spes main koi kami nahin aegi
 The advantage of having Google Drive parvotsapps Backup is that you can open it easily on any smartphone
 agar aapane nayaa phone liya he yaa phir watsap ke liye nae smartphone ko yuj kar rahe hai aise main ye feechar aapke liye phydemand sabit hoga

 byaap banane ke liye watsap ke main menu main ja kar settings par tap karen
 There will be a chat option here, you can select Backup to Google Drive
 yahaan byaap frequency kaa opshan milegaa jise apane hisaab se chun len

 academik galiyaaron main janm shatabdi varsh kii dhooma rahi

 In this compilation, the memoirs of a hundred prominent people who are related to the agnate's contemporary and the agnaya in some form have been included
 yah pustak sansmaranon kii rasaadaaygi vaali koi saamaanya pustak na hokar ek sandarbh granth kii tarah he
 Its 'memoirs' contain memories from the person of the agnostic to literary life, as well as his date-wise biography, list of his works along with the year of publication, and a list of books related to the agnostic
